  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d0cce855-58fa-4192-ab02-335a813afac5'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

While she's instinctively drawn to Gabriel, she's impossibly drawn to Tristan--and confused out of her mind. As she tries to piece together her history Scarlet realizes her past...might just be the death of her.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5055241762170843232"><i>
  <blockquote>Gabriel glanced down. “Seriously, Tristan? You drive around with a trunk full of weapons?”<br/>“Of course.”<br/>“Why?”<br/>“Because I’m the family bad guy</blockquote>
</i><br/><br/>ENCHANTING, SPECTACULAR, GLORIOUS, THRILLING. ONE. OF. THE. BEST SUPERNATURAL BOOKS. I. HAVE. EVER. READ. FORBIDDEN LOVE. TWO BROTHERS. ONE LOVE TRIANGLE.<br/><br/>This book starts with a boom. A fifteen year old girl wakes up in the forest. Alone and scared. How did she get there? Who is she? And why doesn´t she remember anything?<br/><br/>Two years later and she still has </span>
  <span id="freeText5055241762170843232" style="display:none"><i>
  <blockquote>Gabriel glanced down. “Seriously, Tristan? You drive around with a trunk full of weapons?”<br />“Of course.”<br />“Why?”<br />“Because I’m the family bad guy</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />ENCHANTING, SPECTACULAR, GLORIOUS, THRILLING. ONE. OF. THE. BEST SUPERNATURAL BOOKS. I. HAVE. EVER. READ. FORBIDDEN LOVE. TWO BROTHERS. ONE LOVE TRIANGLE.<br /><br />This book starts with a boom. A fifteen year old girl wakes up in the forest. Alone and scared. How did she get there? Who is she? And why doesn´t she remember anything?<br /><br />Two years later and she still has no idea who she is. She is just the girl with amnesia. She lives with her gardian, Laura. She has a best friend, Heather, and she has just started her senior year. She lives a normal life. But she has no idea who she is. Untill one day, when she meets Gabriel Archer. He makes her feel normal. Safe. And not a big freak. But something is of. He has secrets. Does he know who she is? did he knew her before? And what is up with the mysterious guy she´s spotted twice and has been so close to unlock Scarlett´s memories.<br /><br />She and Gabriel slowly starts to build a relationship, and Scarlet gets introduced to a world full of secrets. And SHE is the key to unlock them i<br /><br />Immorttals, semi immortals, the fountain of youth, curses, death.<br /><br />This is a GREAT, FANTASTIC book filled with action and drama. When you start, you won´t be able to put ot down. It bewitches you from page one and every question is answered with another question. Until the end, which is a freaking cliffhanger!!! OMG, the ending! It freaking killed me. I have not been this engrossed in a supernatural book series since Twilight. Thank God book 2 is out and the third is on its way!<br /><br />I loved the authors writing style. It compelled you to the point where you just wanted to keep reading. I loved the characters. I loved simply everything abot this book. And now I only have one question, why on earth have not I read this before?<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote> Before he knew he was immortal. Before life was no longer fragile.<br />Those were the days when life truly meant something.<br /><br />When life was hard but worthwile, and love was valuable because your days were numbered.<br />That was living</blockquote>
</i></span>

If you've just a handful of YA novels you could predict down to the last exclamation point everything that would happen. And I mean <i>everything</i>. <br/><br/>We have the special snowflake...Scarlet<br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Do you think it’s weird to kiss someone you barely know?” <br/>No, it’s perfectly normal and gives us a fantastic excuse to make out. Kiss me!<br/>“Totally weird,” she said, immediately wanting to slap herself. <br/>He no</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText16953464761320065475" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1938954847?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Awry</a>: Book 2 review<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489273615ra/22201496.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dear Lord, from start to finish this was this was severely lacking in originality. If you've just a handful of YA novels you could predict down to the last exclamation point everything that would happen. And I mean <i>everything</i>. <br><br>We have the special snowflake...Scarlet<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Do you think it’s weird to kiss someone you barely know?” <br>No, it’s perfectly normal and gives us a fantastic excuse to make out. Kiss me!<br>“Totally weird,” she said, immediately wanting to slap herself. <br>He nodded slowly. “Me too.” Scarlet’s heart sank a little. Gabriel flashed his dimples. “I guess now I’ve got a good reason to get to know you, don’t I?”<br>Scarlet narrowed her eyes. “Who said I’d let you kiss me even if you got to know me?”<br>He nodded his head with a smile. “Challenge accepted.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489273615ra/22201497.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She's special "just because" and obviously she got the "greek gods" wrapped around her little useless finger. From beginning to end she was just a presence that didn't really add anything to the story unless you count being the reason of the triangle. So I guess there's that. <br><br>Then we have Greek God, the first...Gabriel<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Calm down, Braveheart." Gabriel searched through the weapons. "I'm trying to find something not quite as fatal as...a scythe? Really?"<br>Gabriel held the wicked half-moon blade up and looked at Tristan. "What are you, the Grim Reaper?"<br>"Yes. Yes, Gabriel. I'm the Grim Reaper. You caught me. I drive around in my car full of weapons collecting souls.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489273615ra/22201498.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He's, as you can tell from the blurb, the inconsequential corner of the triangle. The complete opposite of Tristan in the worst ways possible. He's selfish, overbearingly protective, and thinks of Scarlet as some meek, week, vulnerable girl who can't walk into her backyard alone cause she might get lost. The contrast isn't subtle in the least which just seems to detract points for credibility. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489275295ra/22201658.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That's no his job, Scarlet. Get with the program!<br><br>And then we have Greek god, the second...Tristan<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Tristan was silent for a few moments, looking at the leaves before them. "Life isn't about the past and the future. It's about today." He paused. "It's about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. It's moments, you know? Not years. Years aren't what define us.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489274746ra/22201615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So he's obviously the tortured one with a deep soul where everything that spits out his mouth has profound meaning. You're supposed to root for him, in case you haven't gotten the memo. He's the one that truly understands Scarlet and loves her with no conditions or obligations. He's selfless and thinks of Scarlet as someone who can take care of herself, a wildly colored contrast from Gabriel (*ahem* Rhysand and Tamlin all over again). <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489275295ra/22201659.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As for everyone else, they're inconsequential so far. We have the missing parent, Laura, MIA having a life of her own somewhere; the fabulous best friend, Heather, who's only there to make the special snowflake stand out more for being so humble and not caring about her physical appearance; and finally the get out of jail free card, Nate, who just screams "Bonnie" (a character solely used for getting everyone out of trouble).<br><br>So despite being this predictable I'm on my merry way to the second book. It accomplished what it set out to do. In the end, I'm rooting for Tristan, I want Gabriel to find a happy ending somewhere else, and I was to curse to end. What can I say? I'm easy to win over....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448467456ra/17144579.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_242526560" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/242526560" />
    <a title="Bri Martinez •Books and Bri• " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri"><img alt="Bri Martinez •Books and Bri• " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480634774p2/5002397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/242526560?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bri Martinez •Books and Bri• " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bri Martinez •Books and Bri• " href="/user/show/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri">Bri Martinez •Books and Bri• </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri?shelf=want-to-buy">want-to-buy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri?shelf=swoon-worthy-boys">swoon-worthy-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri?shelf=ya-romance">ya-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5002397-bri-martinez-books-and-bri?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer242526560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14524371207092096258">Oh man, I enjoyed this book. I was engrossed the whole time, and each chapter just seemed to get better and better. The writing is phenomenal, the story is original, and Fine’s storytelling is topnotch. And I cannot forget about the cliffhanger! At first, I thought that my e-book was incomplete, but when I found out that was the end, I was partially stupefied and partially enraged. Why of all places did she have to end the book THERE?? <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/326090.gif' width='295' height='256' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Oh, no, she didn’t!</i><br/><br/>As far as cliffhangers are concerned (and</span>
  <span id="freeText14524371207092096258" style="display:none">Oh man, I enjoyed this book. I was engrossed the whole time, and each chapter just seemed to get better and better. The writing is phenomenal, the story is original, and Fine’s storytelling is topnotch. And I cannot forget about the cliffhanger! At first, I thought that my e-book was incomplete, but when I found out that was the end, I was partially stupefied and partially enraged. Why of all places did she have to end the book THERE?? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/326090.gif" width="295" height="256" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Oh, no, she didn’t!</i><br><br>As far as cliffhangers are concerned (and depending on how you feel about them), this book has one of the best/worst cliffhangers I have come across in a while. It definitely has me eagerly waiting for the next book! If you are not a fan, I would advise you to wait to read Anew until the sequel is released. <br><br>While the story itself is amazing, the best part about this book is the characters. The reader cannot help but connect to Scarlet. She has many qualities that I really appreciate in female characters: courage, strength, and the ability to throw some awesome comebacks in a pretty boy’s face. I felt her confusion as she attempts to piece together her past and learn who she is, and I felt her emotional turmoil as she struggled with her growing affection for two brothers. One of the brothers, Gabriel, is an all-around nice guy burdened with a curse that will forever haunt him. His love for Scarlet runs deep and true, and he really cherishes her. Tristan, on the other hand, is the bad boy in their little family. He is dark and mysterious, and even though he hides his true self behind a rough exterior and a mouth that constantly spews insults, he also really cares for Scarlet. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(The guy is willing to die to save her from dying again!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He is a tortured soul, never able to have the one thing he wants the most, and my heart goes out to him. (In fact, he reminds me a lot of Will from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/54144-the-infernal-devices" rel="nofollow noopener">The Infernal Devices series</a> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Clare</a>.) I am definitely rooting for him in this love triangle! I do like Gabriel, but I will always cheer on the dark, tortured man. I guess I am one of the reasons the saying “nice guys finish last” remains true, but I seriously cannot help it! <br><br>I have to commend Fine for her well-written and well-developed love triangle. Very few love triangles are well done. In fact, most are downright torturous. I still think even good love triangles are emotionally grating and frustrating (usually because the guy I like never ‘wins’ and they are chocked full of drama), but at least the men’s proverbial ego wars are absent. I already mentioned this in my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10025305-clockwork-prince" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a>, but I seriously hate it when men fight over a girl through insulting one another, battles of physical prowess, and other creative ways of trying to claim the girl as their own. I think in this case, these ‘contests’ would have been even worse than usual ones since it is a love triangle that involves brothers (I hate when siblings fight). I like the fact that Fine does not include these unnerving elements in her love triangle. It makes the love triangle more bearable (for me, anyway), and it really improves the story instead of hindering it (*cough<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5056084-wings" rel="nofollow noopener">Wings</a>cough*). <br><br>Overall, Anew is a WONDERFUL book, and you should definitely check it out if you haven’t already. I am eagerly anticipating the next book in the series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13334934-awry" rel="nofollow noopener">Awry</a>, which will be released sometime in 2012 (the exact date has yet to be specified). I cannot wait to see what happens after the cliffhanger! The only thing I ask is for, Ms. Fine, is no cliffhanger in the next book! Please! Do not make me summon Conan again (his service fees are ridiculous). <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14524371207092096258" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer473121276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7174842726163356576"><b>Charming, addictive story that completely stole my heart! With a unique and intriguing storyline, likeable characters, and great writing, this was a much needed breath of fresh air!</b><br/><br/><i>Anew</i> starts off with our heroine, Scarlet waking up in the woods with no recollection of who she is or how she got there. Fast forward two years and she is living a comfortable life in small town Georgia just like any other seventeen-year-old girl. A night at the Annual Avalon Kissing Festival changes everything.<br/><br/>When </span>
  <span id="freeText7174842726163356576" style="display:none"><b>Charming, addictive story that completely stole my heart! With a unique and intriguing storyline, likeable characters, and great writing, this was a much needed breath of fresh air!</b><br /><br /><i>Anew</i> starts off with our heroine, Scarlet waking up in the woods with no recollection of who she is or how she got there. Fast forward two years and she is living a comfortable life in small town Georgia just like any other seventeen-year-old girl. A night at the Annual Avalon Kissing Festival changes everything.<br /><br />When she comes face to face with the gorgeous Gabriel Archer, someone who is familiar to her for reasons she doesn’t know, Scarlet is plagued with more questions than she had before. Armed with intense curiosity and a fiery (and pushy) best friend, Scarlet demands to find the answers. Soon it is revealed that Gabriel has a twin brother, Tristan who Scarlet also feels like she has a connection to. As pieces of her past are revealed, it becomes clear that nothing about Scarlet is simple and the secrets of her past go back <i>hundreds</i> of years. <br /><br />This book was so easy to submerse myself in. It’s fast paced, easy to read, and has this effortless feel to it. The writing is simple and smooth with witty dialogue that had me cracking up. The concept of the story is really unique as well. While some things are very obvious, others are not what they seem at all. I kept thinking I knew what was going to happen. Then I’d find out the answers, only to realize that is only the <i>tiniest</i> piece of the puzzle. <br /><br />I have to give an honorable mention to Nate and Scarlet’s best friend, Heather who is hilarious! She’s just the right amount of shallow for it to be funny, but she has a heart of gold and is completely entertaining! <br /><br /><i>“Where did you find him?” <br />“Find him? He’s not a cereal toy, Heather.” <br />“No— but ooh! How awesome would that be? You open a box of Trix and wham! Out pops a hot guy. I would so eat more cereal.” <br /><br />--<br /><br />“Sucking in air, Heather said, “Fluffy—Mrs. Allen’s ferocious dog—chased me all the way down Pine Street trying to tear me to shreds with his razor fangs. I barely got away.”<br />Scarlet scrunched her face. “Isn’t Fluffy a Chihuahua?”<br />Still panting, Heather said, “Yes. A demon-possessed, human-eating Chihuahua.” </i><br /><br />It is told in third person, but from Scarlet, Gabriel and Tristan’s POVs. This format really allows you to get to know the characters individually while also being very easy to follow. I completely fell for these three! Scarlet is independent, resilient, beautiful and strong, a great heroine that I never once got frustrated with. The guys are both great, with very different personalities. Gabriel being the more sweet, safe one and Tristan the more tortured, brooding brother. While this could technically be considered a “love triangle” I really think it isn’t. And if you were to call it one, I’d say it’s probably the least conventional one I’ve ever encountered. To tell you more would be giving too much of the plot away and half the fun is the reveal, so I won’t go there. <br /><br />I loved this book! I can easily see this becoming one of my favorite YA paranormal series in no time. There is so much more than meets the eye and I am dying to find out all the secrets these Archer boys have on Scarlet. After the VERY <u>intense and emotional</u> ending, it is straight on to the next for me!<br /><br /><i>"Life isn't about the past and the future. It's about today." He paused. "It's about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. It's moments, you know? Not years. Years aren't what define us.” </i><br /><br /><b>4 - 4 1/2 stars</b><br /><br /><i>See this review &amp; others at <a href="http://nobsbookreviews.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">No BS Book Reviews</a>. <br />Also 'like' us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/NoBsBookReviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i> ♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="7174842726163356576" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1033232301" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9148206662594313338"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412429080i/11374408._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Look, I know this book has been labelled as <i>Cheesy YA I'm too old for that shit maybe there is instalove in it *gasp*</i>, and you know what? <b>I don't care</b>. <br/><br/>You want to know why? Take a seat. But <i>Watch out!</i> This review may deal with <b>*whisper*</b> feelings. Ugh, I know, big big words.<br/><br/>1) Well, let's meet <b>Tristan</b> first. You know, this guy dressed in black in the beginning. Yep. This one. The <i>broody</i> guy. The one we meet during the first scene, who screams <i>
  <b>"hello, I'm a complete stereotype !!"</b>
</i> - but we </span>
  <span id="freeText9148206662594313338" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412429080i/11374408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Look, I know this book has been labelled as <i>Cheesy YA I'm too old for that shit maybe there is instalove in it *gasp*</i>, and you know what? <b>I don't care</b>. <br><br>You want to know why? Take a seat. But <i>Watch out!</i> This review may deal with <b>*whisper*</b> feelings. Ugh, I know, big big words.<br><br>1) Well, let's meet <b>Tristan</b> first. You know, this guy dressed in black in the beginning. Yep. This one. The <i>broody</i> guy. The one we meet during the first scene, who screams <i>
  <b>"hello, I'm a complete stereotype !!"</b>
</i> - but we love him anyway. And we're right. <i>So. damn. right</i>. Because this guy? He turns out to be so more interesting than he seems at first sight. <b>My little ninja.</b> ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><b>❝Who are you, Tristan?"<br>His eyes looked hopeless as they dove into hers. A moment passed, filled only by the sound of breathing. <br>"Nobody," he said.❞</b><br><br><i>Annnnd</i> here's the crush. <b>*Blush*</b><br><br>✗ This man has <b>daggers</b>. Seriously. <i>You heard me</i>. Freakin' daggers. Actually he owns a room full of weapons - A freakin' ninja. Of course that's totally sexy, isn't it? If you find it weird, just go on the next point. <u>For the others</u> : Of course I'm <i>totally</i> picturing a mix between a pirate and an AC assassin - <i>Hot</i>. <br><br><b>❝Oh, I'm sorry. I'd hate to ruin your <i>date</i> with my inconvenient trying-to-save-Scarlet's-life plan.❞</b><br><br>✗ Want to hear a secret? I give bonus points to the characters whose <b>smart-ass repartees make me giggle</b>. Obviously, Tristan would fill a room with my <i>gold stars</i> (I'm a teacher, remember?). That's simple, he has this awkward way to make others seem dumb. Especially this Gabriel, you know, <i>the other guy nobody cares about.</i> <br><br><b>❝She <i>wasn't</i> a witch." Gabriel sighed.<br>Tristan raised his eyebrows. "She cast a <i>curse</i>, Gabe. That's something <i>witches</i> do. They ride on brooms, play with cats, and curse people.❞</b><br><br>✗ Tristan is so damn awesome that <b>he doesn't need to belittle others</b> to look, well, <i>is perfect a too strong word?</i><br><br>Listen, ladies! Here's the difference between our two male leads - let's discover how they see Scarlett - <br><br><u>Perception #1</u><br><b>❝She was tough. <br>She was brave.<br>Even if she didn't remember she had it, her strength was still there, deep inside her. Which made him kinda proud.❞</b><br><br><u>Perception #2</u><br><b>❝Scarlett was so vulnerable, so weak.❞</b><br><br>Does I need to go into detail? No? That's what I thought.<br><br>✗ Moreover, Tristan manages to be <b>adorable</b>. Really. Sometimes we just want to hug him, because he suffers from the rudeness he has to show. Wow. He was truly <b>heartbreaking</b>.<br><br>✗ <b>To sum up</b>, here's a man with <i>daggers</i>, who lives in a <i>dark basement</i>, whose complex personality offers us a mixture between <b>strength</b> and <b>selflessness</b>. <i>Plus</i>, he's dark-haired and knows how to throw arrows. What - Everybody has his weak spot huh? <br><br>However I wanted to say one thing all the freakin' time. <br><br>☛ Just one thing, Tristan, Tristan, <b>Tristan</b>, <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407482980ra/10728827.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Got it?</b> <br><br>2) What about <b>Scarlet</b>? I must admit that <b>*whisper*</b> I'm often harsh with female leads. Really, I recognize that I'm rapidly annoyed with heroines' monologues but <u>I was pleasantly surprised</u> with this one : her reactions towards the events are always <b>understandable</b>, while believe me, she has to face some really annoying situations. Oh, and she doesn't care how she's dressed. I kind of love her for that because <i>come on</i>, who never wants to slap these heroines who have to save the world and seem to want to live in a <i>let's go dressing for prom</i> day all. the. time. Be careful, I'm not saying she's too much mature, no, her behavior could be the one of a teenager and she's <b>strongly relatable</b> but - <b>she's not obsessed by her looks and... Drum rolls... <u>She asks herself questions and doesn't believe all that some hot guy says to her</u>.</b> And she has a friend. A <i>girl</i> friend. Really. <br><br><b>Amazing right?</b> <br><br>Oh, and she could <i>totally</i> be my friend - <br><b>❝Hello, I'm a stranger. I'm going to kiss you now. Smooch-smooch. Yeah, no thanks.❞</b><br><br>Kissing festival? Eww. <b>Gross.</b><br><br>3) I talked about another male lead, remember? <b>*sigh*</b> <br><br>So, <b>Gabriel</b>,<br><br>Okay, maybe <i>sometimes</i> you're <b>funny</b>.<br><b>❝Yeah, I hate love-sick goobers. They're so <i>happy</i> and <i>annoying</i> and <i>pleasant</i>... always trying to be <i>nice</i> and <i>friendly</i>." He rolled his eyes dramatically. "It's so <i>irritating</i>❞</b><br><br>But where are the daggers? <i>Well?</i> In Tristan's room. Got it. <br><br><u>And you're <b>so f*cking dumb</b></u>.<br><b>❝Dude. Are you going to kill someone tonight?❞</b><br><br><i>Dude</i>, nighttime coffee means serial killer to you? <b>*roll eyes*</b> Be careful people, I might be a serial killer. <b>*nods vigorously*</b> <br><br>As you can guess, I couldn't <i>love</i> Gabriel. That's not my fault, but my heart just <b>can't</b> love <i>everybody</i>, and well, I talked about Tristan remember? Adorable broody Tristan?<br><br>By the way, more I was going further in the story, more I became aware that he was <b>the opposite of Tristan on many ways</b>. <i>Guess what?</i> That's not a good sign. Hello Gabriel! Welcome selfishness! <br><br>4) But a YA wouldn't be a YA without the other characters, you know, the <i>friends</i>. Personally, I have a thing for <b>Nate</b> : hey, the guy has <u>the best voicemail ever</u> and plays videogames. Me loving him is like, destiny. Just kiddin'. Almost. <br><br><b>❝ My bedroom is <i>right</i> next door. How am I supposed to sleep when you're blasting aliens all night?" (...)<br>"First of all," Nate adjusted a speaker and looked back at Gabriel, "the aliens are on <i>my</i> team - so I don't 'blast' them. Second," Nate's eyes grew wide, "you know I have a wicked fear of sleeping underground. Basements are for bats and axe-murders." He looked at Tristan. "No offense".<br>Tristan shrugged. ❞</b><br><br>As for <b>Heather</b>, she appears to be a true friend for Scarlett and by the way, she just won me with the awesome concept she brought - just read and tell me^^<br><br><b>❝No - but ooh! How awesome would that be? You open a box of Trix and wham! Out pop a hot guy! I would so eat more cereal.❞</b><br><br>✎<b>Voilà</b>! I hope my ramblings about these characters will make you want to give it a try. <u>I know what you're thinking though</u> : bloody predictable and unoriginal but let me tell you something (kindly, <i>obviously</i>) : of course some parts remind us of other young adults and this story isn't flawless. I must confess that I had a lot of prejudices - but seriously, Chelsea Fine succeeds in renewing some stereotypes we find in many books and <i>dammit</i>, <b>that page-turner was freakin' refreshing</b>. <b>Funny</b>. I'm gonna definitely read the sequel right now. <i>Even if the blurb just put me on edge.</i><br><br>And you know, <b>Tristan</b> ❤❤ ? <br><br><b>❝Tristan was so weird. And bossy. And... mean. So much for Pancake Tristan. Regular Jerk Tristan was back.❞</b><br><br>Oh, and <u>I almost forgot</u> : <b>no instalove here for me</b>. Nope. <br><br>❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂<br><br>Cross my heart, review soon! But - <br><b>I'm currently in the cave of concentration. Leave a message and I'll call you back in seven-to-ten business days. May the force be with you.</b><br><br>Just - <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412370942ra/11366089.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂❂<br><br>♡♡ Amazing BR with <b>Chelsea, Harriet, Portia, Jen, Laura, Elena and Maria</b> ♡♡<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412274611ra/11349573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9148206662594313338" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_999046300" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/999046300" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/999046300?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13164574-anew">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=alternating-pov">alternating-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=white-knuckle-cliffies">white-knuckle-cliffies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=serious-cliffhanger">serious-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer999046300" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18030896759628368111"><b>*4.5 Stars* </b><br/><br/>And an absolutely SHAMAZING buddy read with all the most wonderful girls- Anna, Harriet, Jen, Portia, Elena, Maria, and Laura ♥ ♥ ♥<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Life isn’t about the past and the future. It’s about today. It’s about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. It’s moments, you know? Not years. Years aren’t what define us.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Wow. Wow. Wow. The vast amount of emotions I felt for this story astounds me. I’m not going to lie-when I was asked to read this, I wasn’t sure how it was going to go. I was </span>
  <span id="freeText18030896759628368111" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 Stars* </b><br><br>And an absolutely SHAMAZING buddy read with all the most wonderful girls- Anna, Harriet, Jen, Portia, Elena, Maria, and Laura ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><b>
  <i>”Life isn’t about the past and the future. It’s about today. It’s about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. It’s moments, you know? Not years. Years aren’t what define us.”</i>
</b><br><br>Wow. Wow. Wow. The vast amount of emotions I felt for this story astounds me. I’m not going to lie-when I was asked to read this, I wasn’t sure how it was going to go. I was happy to be reading with my friends, but I didn’t know if I was going to like it. I’ve had this on my TBR for the longest time but had always skipped over it for whatever reason. Whether it was the cover, the lack of friends having read it, or just the overall description...whatever the reason, I’ve pushed it off. And speaking of one of those issues above…..<b>Why haven’t more people read this?? It’s SO. DAMN. GOOD.</b> For real!! I know it doesn’t seem like much, but this story <b>rocked.</b> Like…really rocked. I am still shocked even a day after finishing. <br><br><b>Heather took a bite of yogurt. “Kristy Stevens told me she saw Gabriel last night, talking to some creepy guy at Freemont Park.”<br>“I thought you hated Kristy Stevens?”<br>“I do.” Heather blinked.<br>“Then why are you talking to her?”<br>“Would you focus here?” Heather pointed her spoon at Scarlet.</b><br><br>So…Scarlet. I love this chick. She wasn’t overly <b>anything.</b> She was…hmmm, how do I say this?? <b>Normal.</b> Yeah, she actually handled things how I would handle them. She wasn’t <i>too</i> proud, she wasn’t overly pushy, she didn’t always trust people just because they told her to, but she did just enough….she followed this fine line that I can totally respect, and it was so refreshing. She wasn’t an unrealistic heroine-she was scared, fierce, protective, funny, kind….and confused, as anyone in her situation would be. <br><br><b>From the corner of her eye, she saw a sad smile tug at his mouth. “Your life has had more meaning than a thousand lives put together.” A few more leaves fell. “You don’t remember how beautiful your life has been, but someday you will. And I,” he cleared his throat, “<i>Gabriel</i> and I won’t let you die this time.” He turned to look at her. “So you have nothing to be afraid of.”</b><br><br>Oooooh and here we go-<b>The boys.</b> Oh. The. Boys. Not one, but two. Two wonderful boys who just happen to protect her at every twist and turn…oh, and did I mention they were <b>twins?</b> <i>Dark haired, dark eyed (okay, okay, one boy has beautiful green eyes…but still), mysterious <b>twins</b></i>. Sound intriguing? Yeah, <b>I thought so.</b> And I don’t know about you guys, but one of them made my heart swell to immeasurable proportions. He was dark, sullen, moody, broody…and completely and utterly <b>heartbroken.</b><br><br><b>It would happen. Tristan couldn’t stop it. And, if he really cared about Scarlet, he shouldn’t stop it. But that didn’t make the thought of them together any less gut-wrenching.<br>Tristan stared blankly at the floor as a piece of his heart broke.<br>His very real, very existent heart.<br><i>And so it begins.</i></b><br><br>Yes, one of the boys has stolen my heart and I don’t think I will ever be able to get it back. Their story, Scarlet and Gabriel and Tristan, is a tragic one. It’s not my story to tell, but just know, not all is as it seems. A completely enthralling and heartfelt story, I fell in love from Tristan’s first POV and on. Their story has been on repeat for centuries, but the love shared between these friends and lovers continues to break their hearts continually. But, even after all these years, they would do anything and everything for one another. And now, even better, we have Heather, Scarlet’s best friend, in the picture. She’s funny, smart, sweet, and loyal-I couldn’t help but to smile every time she said something ludicrous…which was literally all the time. But it was never cheesy or over-the-top. I loved every minute and wouldn’t change a thing. The ending? <b>Epic.</b> Definitely Chelsea Peril approved-which was a totally amazing surprise ;). <br><br><b>His gaze darkened as his eyes left hers and slid down the side of her face to her neck. She could feel them linger there, like her throat-her very pulse-belonged to him and the thought made her heart kick.<br><i>Desire…possession…</i><br>His eyes floated upwards, slowly and methodically, until they reached her lips. She watched him study her mouth and desire sparked in her lower stomach.<br><i>Longing…</i></b><br><br>Many lives have come and gone, but the story always remains the same. One boy’s soul is forever tortured. One girl will always be lost, but her heart tries to find a way. And one boy’s heart has been torn from his body time and again…..and it all makes for a completely <b>forbidden, </b>epic and angsty triangle. <br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491628712i/22430034._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/%20" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="60" width="139" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409285880i/10960212.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><br><br><br>**********************************************<br><br><br><b>Buddy read with some awesome Chicas!!!<br><br>Harriet, Laura, Jen, Elena, Alienortothemoon (Anna, as I call her), Portia, and Maria ♥ </b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_m4n1dkOkGA1rx32kuo1_500_zps49576531.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer18254371859606709514">*1.75/5 stars*<br/><br/>This was just an ok paranormal book. I didn't love or even really like it, but I didn't hate anything about this one either. And in comparison to some other paranormals I've read which made me mad out of my mind because of the double standards and sexism and basically everything - Sweet Evil, Lux, Hush Hush... - this one was pretty pleasant, albeit bland, predictable and over used read. The paranormal world here is just lame, 'cause there's no paranormal world to speak of. The writ</span>
  <span id="freeText18254371859606709514" style="display:none">*1.75/5 stars*<br /><br />This was just an ok paranormal book. I didn't love or even really like it, but I didn't hate anything about this one either. And in comparison to some other paranormals I've read which made me mad out of my mind because of the double standards and sexism and basically everything - Sweet Evil, Lux, Hush Hush... - this one was pretty pleasant, albeit bland, predictable and over used read. The paranormal world here is just lame, 'cause there's no paranormal world to speak of. The writing was just.. eh.. <br /><br />But I did like the dynamic the MC had with Tristan (or should I say Damon??). Love interest number 1 was basically Stefan. The MC Elena and her BFF was basically a TVD season one Caroline.<br /><br />Lets just say someone inspired in TVD quite a lot here...</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1347856655950267647"><b>My goodreads friends, my first 5 shining stars of 2013 goes to....</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402952i/783651._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402952ra/783652.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First of all I want to thank my friend Sarah, who convinced me to read this book A-S-A-P *Heather mode*. Although it wasn’t as soon as possible as I wanted to, I'm glad I read it now when I have all of the series so that I don’t need to wait longer for the sequels. And most of all thank you to Ms. Chelsea Fine who wrote this amazing book that without a doubt will be on my favorite series shelf and I will definitely read it again a</span>
  <span id="freeText1347856655950267647" style="display:none"><b>My goodreads friends, my first 5 shining stars of 2013 goes to....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402952i/783651._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402952ra/783652.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First of all I want to thank my friend Sarah, who convinced me to read this book A-S-A-P *Heather mode*. Although it wasn’t as soon as possible as I wanted to, I'm glad I read it now when I have all of the series so that I don’t need to wait longer for the sequels. And most of all thank you to Ms. Chelsea Fine who wrote this amazing book that without a doubt will be on my favorite series shelf and I will definitely read it again and again and again in the future.<br><br>There are reasons why I loved and enjoyed this book, so let me explain it. Reincarnation and long lost soul mate are one of common stories. But then again I believe there aren't stories that don't influenced by other stories. It authors jobs to make it their own story. I don't mind if the story has similarity and influenced by others as long as it has its originality. Anew is a story like that, though the main theme wasn't new, Ms. Fine brought it differently it makes this reincarnation-long-lost-soul-mate kind of story become her own story. It is kind of fresh story to me. This story has many elements, romance, humor and paranormal but none of it overwhelmed each other. It's perfect and completed those elements.<br><br>The characters are also perfect. No one has bigger portion than another. And most important is I can feel and connect with all of them. I love scarlet &amp; heather friendship, I like their B-F-F *again in heather mode* though heather is kind of noisy-witty bestfriend she completes scarlet personality. She made me look forward her wittiness. She's the one who keep scarlet normal and I can see that they are only 17 year old. I also love the Achers brothers, their look alike with different personality, again it make me see that there aren't similar person, each person is unique and I love the fact their difference influenced their act. Laura and Nate as supporting characters are also great, I look forward for their story and I believe they have bigger role in the sequels.<br><br>Character name is one of my elements to connect to the story. It's weird, I know but I find there are uncommon character name nowadays. If the names suitable with the story I can feel they are really belong to the story thus it makes me connect to the story itself. Gabriel, Tristan, Nathaniel and Scarlet are names from a long time ago. I mean there are classic story and famous people with those names, so it makes sense if they came from hundreds years ago. And Gabriel and Tristan are my most favorite boy names so of course I love it :D<br><br>Although Anew is not pure unpredictable story, I still got surprises here and there. It also made me keep wondering, keep guessing where the story goes and made my heart beat with the characters. But there are issued that I think need to be explained more. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Scarlet can be born in anyplace and any time but the arrow was hidden in the Archers brother's cabin, so it means they used to live in Avalon before, yet I didn’t find about it in this book <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and a part about<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Scarlet death and reborn, the Archers brothers said that Scarlet just vanish and then reappear in a body of 15 years old <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>somehow I can’t picture it in my mind, I really hope Ms. Fine has another explanation other than the way it is because if it is so, I kind of feel she don’t have a reason of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Scarlet’s death and reborn <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>at all. Yet it didn't stop me to give it 5 stars because I still hope there will be more explanation and description in the sequel, after all this is just a prequel, a beginning to the whole story. <br><br>All in all I loved and enjoyed Anew and surely can’t wait for the sequel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13334934.Awry__The_Archers_of_Avalon___2_" title="Awry (The Archers of Avalon, #2) by Chelsea Fine" rel="nofollow noopener"> Awry</a> and [Book: Avow|15711844].<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402952i/783653.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Tristan said, if you had this book, you have to read it today. It's so worth it and I bet you won't regret it. <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_223384077" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/223384077" />
    <a title="Debbie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5098369-debbie"><img alt="Debbie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589209937p2/5098369.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debbie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debbie " href="/user/show/5098369-debbie">Debbie </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Debbie  by: </span>
      <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://chelseafine.blogspot.com/2011/10/anew-cover-reveal.html?spref=tw">http://chelseafine.blogspot.com/2011/...</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5098369-debbie?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5098369-debbie?shelf=on-my-kindle">on-my-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5098369-debbie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5098369-debbie?shelf=series-companion">series-companion</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5098369-debbie?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer223384077" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16559133566687393454">ANEW. What can I say about this novel? Oh, yeah, I LOVE THIS BOOK! Chelsea Fine has just totally set my heart on fire with this amazingly fresh love triangle and storyline. Chelsea Fine has definitely penned a one of a kind story with the gorgeous Archer brothers and forever love of Scarlet. I'm sitting here trying to think how I can give Fine a review that will give her the praise she deserves as the talented writer that she is. And truth is, I will not do this story justice. I can only say I l</span>
  <span id="freeText16559133566687393454" style="display:none">ANEW. What can I say about this novel? Oh, yeah, I LOVE THIS BOOK! Chelsea Fine has just totally set my heart on fire with this amazingly fresh love triangle and storyline. Chelsea Fine has definitely penned a one of a kind story with the gorgeous Archer brothers and forever love of Scarlet. I'm sitting here trying to think how I can give Fine a review that will give her the praise she deserves as the talented writer that she is. And truth is, I will not do this story justice. I can only say I love her writing. She just has a way of bringing a story to life for me with tears, laugher, beautiful romance and a deep, strong storyline. Anew is definitely the right name for Fine's new novel. It’s a new, fresh breath of paranormal romance, with an incredible storyline. And a cliffhanger ending that had me in tears. I thought I would be safe from Chelsea Fine breaking my heart in Anew, after she ripped my heart to pieces in her debut novel Sophie &amp; Carter, but no such luck. Fine has a gift for making my heart feel every tender heart break between her characters. I just might have to email her and ask about Scarlet, Gabriel and Tristan. My heart might not hold out for Awry, the next book in The Archers of Avalon series. <br /><br />Scarlet is seventeen, and two years ago she woke up in the woods of Avalon Georgia with no memory of who or where she came from. Laura, high class business women, becomes her loving guardian and brings Scarlet into her home. Heather becomes Scarlet's best friend and Laura and Heather are trying to help give Scarlet a new, meaningful life again. Scarlet loves these two, but she still feels lost, until this very hot, gorgeous new guy in town talks to her, and his voice sounds familiar to her. Gabriel's voice is a voice that makes Scarlet feel safe, normal, and a voice she can trust. But she just doesn’t know why. She feels this way with Gabriel, but when Scarlet meets Gabriel's mysterious brother, Tristan, her world becomes a whole lot stranger when she hears Tristan voice. It definitely makes her feel things. With the Archers brothers, Scarlet is in for one cursed awakening.<br /><br />I love these two Archer brothers. Their fun, witty, and tough guy relationship with each other is true to how guys act. Well, at least Tristan is tough. Gabriel tries. Chelsea Fine has given these two Archer brothers fantastic personalities. I do love Tristan more, just can't resist that dark bad-boy image . Gabriel and Tristan’s love for Scarlet had me swooning and crying.<br /><br />I also love Heather. She’s the comic relief in this story, and she is what a best friend should be. Heather is not going to let anyone hurt her best friend, not even if Gabriel is one beautiful body that makes a pair of jeans look hot. Heather and Gabriel had me laughing my butt off, especially with them in the classroom. Fine wrote this scene with them perfectly. I could see Heather doing what she did to Gabriel (no spoiler) Girl friends are great. lol<br /><br />Anew is definitely a fresh new take on Paranormal Romance love triangles. I highly recommend Anew as a must read, and I'm begging Chelsea Fine to write the next novel Awry with a fast pen. With that cliffhanger ending, this is going to be an impossible wait! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16559133566687393454" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText6523968623564128534" style="display:none">OMFGOMFGOMFG I FINALLY GOT IT!!!!!!!!!!!<br />ahahahahahahhahahaha eeeeeeeeee omfgomfgomfg cannot express how excited i am... after those quotes and reviews from this book... OMFG!!!!!!!! xD<br /><b>After having read it</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />OMFGOMFGOMFGOMFG.... okayyy .. complaining about the end will come later<br /><br />The story revolves around Scar (Tristan's nickname for her is just too hot to ignore!), Tristan (green eyed twin) and Gabriel (brown eyed twin)<br />I really liked Scar, she was sarcastic and funny and didn't jump to conclusions too quickly like some. <br />I loved her meeting with Gabriel at the kissing festival !!! -for Scar this is <b>'like Valentine’s Day. On crack.'</b> it was different from anything you see in England and actually sounded fun! Her meeting with Gabriel and their blossoming love was nice but my heart was already possessed by the hot guy sporting a black tee and baseball cap who was staring at her at the kissing festival( TRISTAN ). <br /><br />Gabriel was really charming at first but for some reason he came across as a little selfish.. but i think i just over analysed some stuff. He's definitely boyfriend material and someone you would snuggle up with and watch a movie.<br /><br />but Tristan, his sexier green-eyed twin, is the sort of guy you'd have a hot make-up session with on the coach and totally bury the tv remote. He's sarcasm and 'keep Scar safe' thing is heart warming and i feel myself start to hate Gabriel for touching his girl! Scar's connection with Tristan is deep, really deep... the sexual tension they share is so hawwwwwwwt it makes me wanna scream and pull out my hair in a bid to get him to kiss her already!!<br /><br />His relationship with Gabriel is sooo... (a word that means you just wanna smile!). Their little banter while Gabriel spies Tristan's truck full of weapons was really funny and made me forget my frustration on who the hell the creepy stalker was.<br /><br />Everything about Tristan wanted me to swap places with Scar sooo much.. especially her description of his bed. 'The post screamed man while the bedding whispered woman' --- c'mon Chelsea Fine you are killing us here!!!!!! her writing is so wonderfully hypnotic i want more... need more..... like RIGHT NOW! and the ending... [okay i am trying to write this without giving the plot away ( i realise i haven't done that successfully at all)] OMFG what is the ending supposed to mean.... does she die? Is the curse broken? where the hell is the fountain? argggggggg please hurry Ms Fine!!!!!<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>BIG SPOILER : </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />ohhh and the tattoo on Tristans body...... ohmagawwwwwd .. did Scar and Tristan have sex?! <span id="freeTextContainer9817948696834171765">What an awesome story! It was so beautiful, kind of a beautiful sad. The characters are in pain, but you still love it all the same. The originality of the story line hooked me from the very beginning and kept me up well past midnight!<br/><br/><br/><br/>I hardly ever believe in love triangles, not many authors can pull it off. It’s always painfully obvious who the leading lady should be with. But this one was different. I can see how Scarlet might be confused about how she feels. One brother loves her utterly and </span>
  <span id="freeText9817948696834171765" style="display:none">What an awesome story! It was so beautiful, kind of a beautiful sad. The characters are in pain, but you still love it all the same. The originality of the story line hooked me from the very beginning and kept me up well past midnight!<br /><br /><br /><br />I hardly ever believe in love triangles, not many authors can pull it off. It’s always painfully obvious who the leading lady should be with. But this one was different. I can see how Scarlet might be confused about how she feels. One brother loves her utterly and completely and gives her what she needs. The other is incredibly complicated. But whoever said the road to true love was easy? I know who I would choose, but Scarlet is young and a litte naïve and is at a disadvantage of not knowing what the hell is going on right from the start. And it doesn’t help her that the boys are keeping secrets. But in the end I think she realised who she is meant to be with. But if they are to have any chance to be together, they must first break the curse. Which I CANNOT wait for!! The sexual tension between Scarlet and one of the boys is so intense I had to take a minute to calm down, my heart was literally racing! It’s a wonder I didn’t die from heart failure.<br /><br /><br /><br />At the end I cried and cried and cried. My heart simply bled. But like I said, it was a beautiful sad. I loved it. It was an incredible climax. And I CANNOT wait for the sequel! Please hurry Ms Fine!!!<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12130589193516069174">Meh. I give this one a 2,5 stars rating. It's really not a bad book : I enjoyed the writing and (some) of the characters (namely Heather and Tristan, the latter being the main reason I kept reading, I thought that Gabriel, the main "love interest" was boring) but I felt like nothing of real significance happened.   <span id="freeText12130589193516069174" style="display:none">Meh. I give this one a 2,5 stars rating. It's really not a bad book : I enjoyed the writing and (some) of the characters (namely Heather and Tristan, the latter being the main reason I kept reading, I thought that Gabriel, the main "love interest" was boring) but I felt like nothing of real significance happened. Seriously, there was little action, the big reveal took forever to unravel and that REALLY frustrated me. Scarlett started off as a strong character but started annoying me once she learned about her special "condition". I don't even know how to explain it really...i was just expecting MORE. More action, more drama, more romance, more excitement....(also I kept hoping this would be a retelling of the arthurian legend and was actually disappointed when I found out it wasn't. Ridiculous I know. But in my defense, the book IS called the archer of Avalon ;D)<br /><br />This one could have been a real page-turner (short chapters, great opening scene, a swoon-worthy boy) but unfortunately it fell flat for me. However, I will pick up the sequel when it comes out mostly because I really want to know what happens to Tristan.</span>

<div id="review_846788203" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846788203" />
    <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog"><img alt="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576986930p2/28353412.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846788203?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog">Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18897426-anew">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=giggleworthy">giggleworthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=romance-forbidden-or-starcrossed">romance-forbidden-or-starcrossed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=love-makes-my-heart-happy">love-makes-my-heart-happy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=romance-hate-to-love">romance-hate-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=bad-boys-i-love">bad-boys-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=sigh-bbf">sigh-bbf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846788203" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5241146321736513553"><b>Buddy read with Chelsea, Harriet, Laura, Alienortothemoon ♥, Portia, Elena & Maria</b><br/><br/>I was hooked from the very first page. Anew sunk it’s claws deep into my heart, and I am still in shock over how much this book made me feel. The sarcastic humor had me constantly laughing, the undercurrent of mystery and love had me turning the pages as fast as possible and the characters warmed and angered my heart. Anew completely captivated me, and I never wanted to leave the town of Avalon.<br/><br/><b>It would happen. Tri</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5241146321736513553" style="display:none"><b>Buddy read with Chelsea, Harriet, Laura, Alienortothemoon ♥, Portia, Elena &amp; Maria</b><br><br>I was hooked from the very first page. Anew sunk it’s claws deep into my heart, and I am still in shock over how much this book made me feel. The sarcastic humor had me constantly laughing, the undercurrent of mystery and love had me turning the pages as fast as possible and the characters warmed and angered my heart. Anew completely captivated me, and I never wanted to leave the town of Avalon.<br><br><b>It would happen. Tristan couldn’t stop it. And, if he really cared about Scarlet, he shouldn’t stop it. But that didn’t make the thought of them together any less gut-wrenching.<br>Tristan stared blankly at the floor as a piece of his heart broke.<br>His very real, very existent heart.<br><i>And so it begins.</i></b><br><br>Hope, mystery, love, despair, and at the bottom of it all is a curse. Three curses to be exact. This will become Scarlett’s life but she doesn’t know that yet, or more correctly stated, she doesn’t remember her past yet. Scarlett wakes up in the middle of the forest alone and terrified out of her mind. The only thing she can remember is her name. The rest is blank, completely blank. Fast forward two years and she has settled into a nice, safe life. She is lucky. But her world is about to be shaken and she will have two boys to thank for that. Gabriel has a voice that she recognizes, that she knows but can’t place. While getting close to Gabriel, she discovers that he has kept his brother, Tristan, a secret. Why would he do that? And why does she feel such a strong pull to Tristan? What other secrets are they keeping from her?<br><br><b>Wind blew across the porch, lifting a strand of her dark hair and blowing it across her face. A rush of memories – shoved to the depths of his soul in punishment – broke free and flooded his mind as he stared at her.<br>Memories of love. Memories of life. Memories of torment…death… (Tristan)</b><br><br>For me, there is no competition. There is no debate over which Archer brother is the right one for Scarlett. Tristan completely won over my heart and soul. His dark, sarcastic humor was intoxicating. His selflessness and bravery was endearing. And his love and interactions with Scarlett were incredibly butterfly inducing. Even when he was being a jerk, I couldn’t get enough of him. Tristan is everything I love, and so much more.<br><br><b>Scarlet eyed the brothers for a moment.<br>Trust her gut? Her gut was currently telling her to run her hands through Tristan’s dark hair. She wasn’t so sure her gut was reliable.</b><br><br>Scarlet is sassy, tough and brave. Throughout each pitfall and each emotional memory, she tried to stand strong. She wasn’t going to let some curse get the better of her. I loved her attitude, but one thing drove me a little crazy this second time around. Her ability to become close to Gabriel. I understand he made her feel normal and safe but honestly, I just can’t stand behind Gabriel. He was so vanilla. I never felt any passion or lust between him and Scarlet. And some of his actions bothered me. They say love makes you do desperate things, but for me, he takes it to a level I wasn’t comfortable with. To put it bluntly, there were a few times I wanted to punch him in the throat, make him disappear, and bring Tristan into the picture. I’m clearly not biased or anything! But in all due honesty, Gabriel wasn’t that bad. But the problem for me was that he wasn’t Tristan. He could never be Tristan.<br><br><b>He looked haunted. Pained.<br>Her heart thrummed as she felt something sorrowful grow inside of her. Heavy and warm and full of regret, it whispered something to her soul. Something powerful. Something sad.<br>Something Scarlet couldn’t remember.</b><br><br>Anew mesmerized me. While the mystery unfolded, I found myself falling head over heels for a tortured soul and rooting on a new favorite heroine. The side characters were quirky, fun and memorable. And the storyline left me laughing, breathless and the feeling that my heart was going to explode out of my chest. I can’t wait to see how the rest of the series progresses, because I may have just found a new favorite series!<br><br><b>From the corner of her eye, she saw a sad smile tug at his mouth. “Your life has had more meaning than a thousand lives put together.” A few more leaves fell. “You don’t remember how beautiful your life has been, but someday you will.” (Tristan)</b><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i> <br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287496i/17673736._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b> </b>
</u><br><a title="Facebook" href="https://www.facebook.com/starcrossedbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055977i/15660595.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_688292349" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/688292349" />
    <a title="Lucy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16396455-lucy"><img alt="Lucy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475433960p2/16396455.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/688292349?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucy" href="/user/show/16396455-lucy">Lucy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer688292349" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7066304116083332180">*4.75/5*<br/><br/>Before I begin to ramble about this amazing book, <i>
  <u>let me tell you one thing:</u>
</i> <b>I do not want write this review <u>right now</u>…</b> <i>Why?</i> <b>Not because I don’t have much to say about it</b> (yeah in fact I could talk about the plot and the characters, especially TRISTAN for hours…), no it’s because <b>I so want to read the sequel straight away that I have trouble to think about something else!</b><br/><br/><i>Having say that</i>, <u>it’s my duty</u> to tell you <b>why this book is so awesome</b> and <b>make sure everyone who will read this re</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7066304116083332180" style="display:none">*4.75/5*<br><br>Before I begin to ramble about this amazing book, <i>
  <u>let me tell you one thing:</u>
</i> <b>I do not want write this review <u>right now</u>…</b> <i>Why?</i> <b>Not because I don’t have much to say about it</b> (yeah in fact I could talk about the plot and the characters, especially TRISTAN for hours…), no it’s because <b>I so want to read the sequel straight away that I have trouble to think about something else!</b><br><br><i>Having say that</i>, <u>it’s my duty</u> to tell you <b>why this book is so awesome</b> and <b>make sure everyone who will read this review</b> will add “Anew” on their TBR shelf! <i>What kind of blogger I would be otherwise?</i><br><br>So, I think you <u>did understand</u> that <b>I loved almost all about Chelsea Fine’s novel</b>, starting with the plot. <br><br><b>I must admit the beginning let me confused.</b> Kissing Festival? <i>Really?</i> <u>Definitely gross.</u> My first thought was: OMG in what kind of world everyone’s kissing strangers just for fun? In fact, <b>it was only an excuse to introduce our heroin and prove Chelsea Fine’s humor…</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273489i/13479152._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><u>So go forward</u>, because <b>this story is really a little nugget</b> which make my heart beats faster all along the pages. <b>I have to say Chelsea Fine got me at the word <u>“curse”</u>.</b> Sometimes I really don’t need more than <u>ONE idea</u> <b>to keep me on the edge.</b> And Chelsea Fine did that <u>particularly well</u> because <b>she managed to surprise me at each chapter with her marvelous ideas.</b> <i>At first,</i> you believe everything is quite simple but <i>let me advise you and don’t let the author fool you</i> because <b>she definitely knows how to keep her cards close to her chest.</b> <u>To conclude</u>: be prepared, you will not be able to put this book down until the end!<br><br>But, <i>being honest, what definitely won my heart?</i> <b>The characters.</b><br> <br>Okay, <i>
  <u>being really honest,</u>
</i> <b>TRISTAN</b> won my heart. <i>Oh.My.Gosh.</i> I don’t even know <u>where</u> to start with him. <b>I might tell you he is a part of a love triangle</b> but <i>
  <u>hey guys</u>
</i>, don’t hurl at me about that because <i>in my opinion</i> there is not really a love triangle in this story. <u>For me</u>, <b>Tristan is the love interest.</b> I know I could be wrong but still, in any case, <b>he is MY love interest.</b> <u>In short</u>, he is all I love in a man character: <b>mysterious, broody, moody and definitely swoon-worthy!</b> <i>*Whisper* Don’t tell it to my husband but I totally fall for him. <u>Hard.</u></i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273489i/13479153._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So, and <i>in order to keep the things clear</i>: <u>on the one hand</u>, <b>we have Tristan, the bad but oh, so sexy brother who made me collapse more than one time</b> (yeah literally, I must admit tattoos drive me crazy… yeah I know: cliché…), and <u>on the other hand</u> <b>we have the boring brother: Gabriel.</b> <i>Don’t get me wrong,</i> <b>Gabriel is quite great. <u>From time to time</u></b>. He is kind and helpful but even if he shares the same DNA with his brother, <b>he can’t compete.</b> Besides, <b>I found him pretty selfish with Scarlet…and not really brave... </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273489i/13479154._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <u>By the way</u>
</i>, it’s about time to talk about our heroin, <i>don’t you think?</i> <b>I can’t say I totally adored her in the beginning.</b> She was a bit naïve and kind of annoying at time because I really felt she was not wondering the right questions. <u>However</u> I knew immediately Scarlet had a huge potential. <b>She is the kind of heroin you learn to love because even if she is far from flawless, she is decisive, sensitive and quite badass</b> around the end of this first novel.<u> Above all</u>, <b>she doesn’t trust guys only because they’re handsome</b> and that's a really good point! <i>Go girl, you don't need guys for take care of yourself! Yeah Gabe you're my target!!</i> Besides, Scarlet lost her memory so I think she's not really herself in Anew. <b>I'm pretty sure I could talk more about her when I will review the next installment...</b> So we'll see...<br><br>Finally, <b>I need to say some words about Heather.</b> The <b>fun and kind of crazy</b> Scarlet's best friend. Like Tristan, <b>she totally amazes me!</b> Seriously, I want the same best friend, she is absolutely wonderful!! <b>I think I could fullfill a plain notebook with her quotes</b> because her feedbacks are always totally hilarious! <i>
  <u>Takes this one for perfect example:</u>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273489i/13479155._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Well</i>, I can't believe I finally finished writing this review!! <u>It means ONE thing</u>: <b>I can resume my reading with the sequel!!!</b> See you soon about that, guys!!!<br><br>(<u>Last thought:</u> you must wonder why I rate this only 4.75/5... Just because I know, from a reliable source, <b>Awry is even better</b>!!)</span>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972017-lalaine-myficbookreviews?shelf=my-favorite-reads">my-favorite-reads</a>
