        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247318134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6849675891983493069"><br/>"What was the point of living if only to die? Her eyes still closed, Scarlet listened to the forest."<br/><br/>Dark, cute, heartbreaking and hot hot hot immortals! I want more!<br/><br/>I EFFIN LOVED THIS BOOK! I was kind of avoiding books about souls reincarnation thingo these days,not many authors can pull this off. But this book was actually quite a pleasant surprise! A romance that will pull at your heartstrings. Chelsea Fine did an amazing job weaving a beautiful (but tinged with sadness) story about a mysteri</span>
  <span id="freeText6849675891983493069" style="display:none"><br />"What was the point of living if only to die? Her eyes still closed, Scarlet listened to the forest."<br /><br />Dark, cute, heartbreaking and hot hot hot immortals! I want more!<br /><br />I EFFIN LOVED THIS BOOK! I was kind of avoiding books about souls reincarnation thingo these days,not many authors can pull this off. But this book was actually quite a pleasant surprise! A romance that will pull at your heartstrings. Chelsea Fine did an amazing job weaving a beautiful (but tinged with sadness) story about a mysterious girl who knows nothing of her past but her name, Scarlet Jacobs.<br /><br />I was completely engrossed with ANEW. This book is on third-person narrative of multiple characters, that's Scarlet, Gabriel and Tristan. Characters were great, they have actual depth and personality. I was mesmerized by their story and anxious for them. And man, the love triangle, it was refreshing and so good, well executed. One thing I don't like about Scarlet was she can be a kill joy sometimes (cant blame her though, not having a memory at all suck) but a great strong character nonetheless. And this twins Gabriel and Tristan were so cool and funny and sexy! Gabriel is a sweet, jolly guy while Tristan is a broody, mysterious kind of guy, its because he has a reason to be, I adore him. Loved it when the brothers bicker with each other, and also Nate and Heather such a cute and great friends.<br /><br />Plot twist was great and unpredictable, mystery has kept me from guessing, the storyline was more of revealing the curse, and Scarlet meeting the boys, the complicated love, pain, life and death and a great friendship and a little bit of memory flashbacks. Great for para and romance lover. But there's still some questions that needs answers and I guess it would be on the second book .And the ending! OMG breath-taking! I cried! It was a good darn CLIFFHANGER! I really want more! *dies*<br /><br />Quotes I loved:<br /><br /><br /> Tristan was silent for a few moments, looking at the leaves before them. "Life isnt about the past and the future. Its about today." He paused. "Its about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. Its moments, you know? Not years. Years arent what define us."<br /><br /> "Knowing death is nearby gives you a chance to live...deliberately." -Tristan <br /><br /> " Before life was no longer fragile.<br /> Those were the days when life truly meant something.<br /><br /> When life was hard but worthwile, and love was valuable because your days were numbered.<br /> That was living." - Tristan</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15701576625342830890">I have read a lot of books throughout the years and I came to a point where not much surprises me or intrigues me but I have to say this.... Holy cow, Chelsea Fine had me intrigued about her story and asking myself how the story would unfold. <br/>Starting with the characters names, loved them, loved their names, their personalities, their vulnerability, in fact I am very much in love with them, even Nate owns a special place in my heart now and I want a happy ending for everybody.<br/>About the plot, Che</span>
  <span id="freeText15701576625342830890" style="display:none">I have read a lot of books throughout the years and I came to a point where not much surprises me or intrigues me but I have to say this.... Holy cow, Chelsea Fine had me intrigued about her story and asking myself how the story would unfold. <br />Starting with the characters names, loved them, loved their names, their personalities, their vulnerability, in fact I am very much in love with them, even Nate owns a special place in my heart now and I want a happy ending for everybody.<br />About the plot, Chelsea managed to bring something new, Scarlet wakes up in the middle of a forest and had no memories at all, she only knows her name and her age. Despite her believing she is a normal girl, she is way much more than that and after going to a Kissing Festival (awesome idea for a festival by the way) she meets two boys who will captivate her attention and her heart in completely different ways. <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Scarlet, Tristan, Gabe and Nate have a curse to deal with and they are against time as Scarlet's life depends on getting this curse broken and on top of this they will find their hearts entangled and no matter what, someone will have their heart broken.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I really recommend Anew to be read, I really enjoyed it and the cliffhanger is a punch in the face. <br /><br />I also must add that the price of this book is very welcoming, Chelsea is definitely a humble writer and I admire her even more for that.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer311895596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8417623550066577841">When i read finished reading this book, all that came to mind was "OHMIGODOHMIGOD" I seriously was dying to get my hands on the next one. I loved it so much i had to tell someone about it so i woke up my cousin and told here about the whole novel. Seriously. The forbidden romance, and the love triangle, the crazy, witty bestfriend, and the boy, in my book all equal to a great novel! So if you enjoy romantic mysterious books, go buy this one! XOXO</span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_585633461" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/585633461" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17688793-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601659534p2/17688793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/585633461?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/17688793-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17688793-laura?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17688793-laura?shelf=fantasy-sci-fi">fantasy-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17688793-laura?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17688793-laura?shelf=fav-characters">fav-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer585633461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4582722263335297019"><b>October 2nd, 2014:<br/>Doing a buddy read with the lovelies Chelsea, Elena, Jen, Harriet, Maria, Portia and Alienortothemoon ♥</b><br/><br/><b>4,5 his-jaw-line-is-delicious-stars!</b><br/><br/>Sigh.. this was beautiful! I forgot how easy it is to get lost in the world of the Archer of Avalon. Everything about it - the characters, the plot, the twists - it's all so much fun! That's exactly what <i>Anew</i> is, an extremely fun read!<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"Life isn't about the past and the future. It's about today. It's about five minutes from now and two sec</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4582722263335297019" style="display:none"><b>October 2nd, 2014:<br>Doing a buddy read with the lovelies Chelsea, Elena, Jen, Harriet, Maria, Portia and Alienortothemoon ♥</b><br><br><b>4,5 his-jaw-line-is-delicious-stars!</b><br><br>Sigh.. this was beautiful! I forgot how easy it is to get lost in the world of the Archer of Avalon. Everything about it - the characters, the plot, the twists - it's all so much fun! That's exactly what <i>Anew</i> is, an extremely fun read!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Life isn't about the past and the future. It's about today. It's about five minutes from now and two seconds ago. It's moments, you know? Not years. Years aren't what define us."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>In my opinion the characters contribute most to make this story so extraordinary and fun. First off all, there's <b>our heroine Scarlet</b>. Scarlet's feisty, <s>a little</s> stubborn, loyal and generally a strong heroine. Still recovering from waking up in the woods with amnesia two years earlier, she's trying to find her way and figure out who she is in this world she woke up in without memories. I especially like how while she allows herself to be scared and seek solace from Gabriel or Heather, she never lets it completely get to her. Also, I loved that she still made her own decisions even though both Gabriel and Tristan would gladly do them for her and kept bossing her around a bit. But she never gives in to them and does what she thinks is right. It makes her a really likable heroine in my eyes.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Tristan lived in a dark basement. Of course.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Then, there's also <b>Gabriel</b>. The first of the Archer brothers she meets in Avalon. Gabriel is a sweet guy who immediately makes her feel normal again, after two years of a life being everything but normal. Naturally she's drawn to that and the weird familiarity she feels every moment she spends with him. <br>I sort of liked Gabriel the first time around, though of course he's always in the shadow of his simply more interesting brother, but this time, knowing what I do about their history, he made me extremely mad! I won't go into it because of possible spoilers, but know that I think he's being so extremely selfish this whole time. I do feel bad for him because his part of the curse really does suck a lot, but compared to what Tristan and Scarlet go through.. his curse just pales in comparison. And the way he deals with everything drives me nuts. He never helps Tristan in his attempts to end the curse, but always makes him the bad guy, although he doesn't even know what his brother is doing! He's just making his assessments based on assumptions and it makes me so mad! And I won't even go into the whole Gabriel-Scarlet-Tristan thing because I'd end up rambling forever and spoiling everything. I think it's time to move on.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"All these arrows are sharp and have blood on them."<br>"Yes, well. I left my cotton candy arrows at home next to my teddy bear."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Moving on to <b>Tristan</b>!! My baby. My everything. Tristan is such a tortured soul and I love it! He's moody, sometimes kinda mean, usually a jerk and extremely loyal if you look under the layers of assoholery he hides behind. Especially already knowing his reasons during this read, I felt for him so much. I hated having to watch him watch Gabriel date Scarlet and swoop into her life while he can't do anything about it. His situation is so damn fucked up and it's just not fair. But at the same time because of all that, we get to see his jerk-side and I'm not complaining. Because jerk Tristan is soo hot, especially since it's all to keep a certain someone safe. ♥ Tristan is one of my favorite heros ever, just so you know. I think reading this series would be so worth it, if only because you'd get to meet him! He's wonderful in every single one of his incarnations. Regular Jerk Tristan. Moody Tristan. Pancake Tristan. I don't care - I want them all!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"You think I hate you?"<br>Scarlet shrugged. "Do you?"<br>Tristan looked at the floor, then at the wall, and finally at Scarlet. "No."<br>Their eyes locked again and Scarlet's chest tightened. He was so beautiful and guarded, like he had a thousand secrets and no one to trust.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Of course while I was busy swooning and gushing, I completely forgot to mention how funny Tristan could be. Seriously. Especially the dialogues with Gabriel are hilarious. Tristan acting like he was doing something completely normal, even when he was leaving the house in black Ninja attire with a sword strapped to his back. And Gabriel being completely exasperated with him pretty much 24/7. It's all extremely entertaining and I could read about them all day long. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"We're <i>not</i> going to kill that guy."<br>"We might."<br>"Tristan, that's homicide."<br>"It's self defense."<br>"It's not self defense. He didn't come after you."<br>"But he came after Scarlet. And technically, Scarlet is a piece of me. So yeah, it's self defense."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>One simply cannot argue with Tristan. He will always have the upper hand. You can just give up right now. Here's one more, for good measure. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Gabriel stared. "I can<i>not</i> believe you actually did that."<br>"Maybe if you weren't such a pretty boy you could do it too."<br>"Just because I don't want to track down crazy people in the woods on a full moon doesn't mean I'm a pretty boy."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Aren't they amazing? And speaking of amazing, I still haven't talked about <b>my favorite zombie slaying nerd-guy Nate.</b> While he doesn't have too many scenes in <i>Anew</i>, he still owns the ones he does have. Seriously, I absolutely love that guy. He knows basically everything, is Tristan and Gabe's <s>servant</s> go-to guy and handles every single one of their crises. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Can I get you anything? Water? Juice?"<br>"Do you have Lucky Charms?"<br>"Uh, maybe. Do you <i>want</i> Lucky Charms?"<br>"If you've got them."<br>Scarlet smiled and led him into the kitchen to make him a bowl of cereal like he was a four-year old or something.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>You simply HAVE to love Nate. Everything else is impossible. I can't wait to read more about his awesomeness in the next two books, because trust me, there's a lot of it in there. ♥<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Nate held his hand in the air. "Good to see you, Scarlet. High-five!"<br>She awkwardly high-fived him. "Do we... know each other?"<br>"Yep. You just don't remember me. But no worries. I'm super awesome and you're going to love me."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Look at me only rambling about the characters! And I haven't even talked about <b>Heather</b> yet. Heather is <b>Scarlet's crazy best friend</b> who frequently talks in text language and is generally a little insane. But she's an extremely loyal friend and probably the best thing that happened to Scarlet after waking up with amnesia. She adds even more charm and funny scenes to these books and I love her for it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Of course not. She's not a cry-baby. She's <i>fine</i>. She's just...far away, you know?" She snapped his fingers in his face. "So fix it. I need my best friend back. And also, I need her to start wearing matching socks. Today, she had on a white one, and an <i>off</i>-white one." She tossed her hands in the air. "Unacceptable."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>So, as you can see, I have a thing for basically all of the characters. But while they make up a huge part of why I love this book, doesn't mean the book has nothing else to offer. The story world Chelsea Fine created is very special and definitely unique in the YA genre. There are curses and fountains of youth and crazy ash people, all for your pleasure. I absolutely love all the paranormal bits Fine spun into her story. Also, there's so much mystery. The reader's left to figure out what exactly happened in the past with Gabriel, Tristan and Scarlet and how it all affected them and their actions. Even the second time reading this, I love all this mystery, although I mostly know what happened, because now I completely get why everyone is acting the way they do. I can't wait to re-read the next two books when the real action will happen. ♥<br><br><b>READ THESE BOOKS!</b><br><br><br><b>Pre re-read:</b> I'M SO EXCITED FOR MY TRISTAN BABY, YOU HAVE NO IDEA! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384210850ra/6815669.gif" width="350" height="219" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I know, I know. But seriously, I love Tristan.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398625059ra/9442581.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>April 19th, 2013:</b> I loved loved loved it!! It's a really unique story that has so much potential! I can't wait to read <i>Awry</i>! - 4.5 stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4582722263335297019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/262566425" />
    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/262566425?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=action-romance-hot-stuff">action-romance-hot-stuff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=paperback-or-hc-i-own">paperback-or-hc-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=fantasy-romance-mystery-the-whole">fantasy-romance-mystery-the-whole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=fave-books-of-2012">fave-books-of-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=books-of-2012">books-of-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262566425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10092313504299692726"><br/>
  <i>***I would like to thank Chelsea Fine and her publisher Karen Gray for providing a review copy in exchange for a honest review.***</i>
<br/><br/>Ever since I heard about <i>Anew</i>, I couldn’t wait to dig into it. I was drawn to the three things that everyone falls for when reading an engaging and fresh paranormal YA book - the mystery, the exquisitely developed characters and the romance - and they definitely did not disappoint! It had a very unique twist to the paranormal aspect, which is never a bad thing, so</span>
  <span id="freeText10092313504299692726" style="display:none"><br />
  <i>***I would like to thank Chelsea Fine and her publisher Karen Gray for providing a review copy in exchange for a honest review.***</i>
<br /><br />Ever since I heard about <i>Anew</i>, I couldn’t wait to dig into it. I was drawn to the three things that everyone falls for when reading an engaging and fresh paranormal YA book - the mystery, the exquisitely developed characters and the romance - and they definitely did not disappoint! It had a very unique twist to the paranormal aspect, which is never a bad thing, so I was instantly hooked from the first to the last page. The story was full of gut-wrenching action, adventure, intrigue and thrilling romance. I couldn’t put it down. A well thought-out idea by Ms. Fine and just as brilliantly executed - <i>Anew</i> will definitely keep you at the edge of your seat!<br /><br />The one thing that I was blown away by was the storyline for this book. It was very original and completely fascinating. Above all, the way Ms. Fine crafted the idea, especially, had me impressed. This idea of an unknown past, an ancient curse, having a hole in your memory and your only connection to those memories: 2 guys - makes for one very compelling novel. With new twists and turns around every corner, the fast-moving plot will have you pulling your hair out, trying to figure out the mystery of Scarlet’s lost past. The plot was to-the-point, (I loved that!) - making the story an overall engaging read.<br /><br />Like previously mentioned, the characters in <i>Anew</i> were amazing. There is just no other way to describe them. The characters had depth and the fact that they were NOT perfect, was the icing on the cake. Scarlet, Tristan and Gabriel all had palpable flaws - making it easier for readers to sympathize for them <i>or</i> with them. This is also clearly seen through the changes in points of view. Getting snippets of Tristan’s or Gabriel’s perspective throughout the story, really helped to understand the “whys” of their decisions. Not a fan of more than one points of view in a story, the change in perspective, surprisingly enough, I found did not overwhelm the story. The transitions from one character to another were smooth and very well done - which I greatly appreciated.<br /><br />As far as relationships go, Ms. Fine did a brilliant job in developing a relationship among the brothers and Scarlet, that surpassed the “rules” of a normal love triangle. Each brother has a very distinct relationship witch Scarlet - which not all borders on just being romantic. Scarlet and Tristan have a lot of chemistry between them and they have that instant connection - whereas, Gabriel is more of the best friend type. While all signs do point to Tristan as the final outcome of this relationship, the set up of this love triangle proves (to say the least) to be unpredictable and the happy ever after remains to be seen - which is probably why I wasn’t cringing at the romance.<br /><br /><i>Anew</i> was, without a doubt, a highly addictive and enjoyable read. With a mind blowing ending, that leaves you with more questions than answers (not a bad thing), I am anxious to get my hands on the next installment, <i>Awry</i>. A fantastic start to the series, <i>Anew</i> was a definite page turner. To say I am impressed with Ms. Fine’s work, would most certainly be an understatement.<br /><br /><b>My Rating:</b> 5 of 5 HEARTS!!!<br /><br />This review is also posted @ <a href="http://loveaffairwithabookreviews.blogspot.ca/2012/10/review-anew-by-chelsea-fine-giveaway.html#more" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary Love Affair</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="10092313504299692726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer254749076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15263687995533117671">WoW! What a way to begin the brand new year with an awesome book that had me hooked from beginning to end. For the life of me though I can't believe I put off reading this book for so long. I'm not really sure why but I thank God that I decided to pick it up, all because of my groups A-Z Challenge…wooohoo. What I loved most was how unique and refreshing the storyline was on a genre that has been done so many ways to Sunday. I really was captivated and drawn into this paranormal world that felt s</span>
  <span id="freeText15263687995533117671" style="display:none">WoW! What a way to begin the brand new year with an awesome book that had me hooked from beginning to end. For the life of me though I can't believe I put off reading this book for so long. I'm not really sure why but I thank God that I decided to pick it up, all because of my groups A-Z Challenge…wooohoo. What I loved most was how unique and refreshing the storyline was on a genre that has been done so many ways to Sunday. I really was captivated and drawn into this paranormal world that felt so real and true. <br><br>Anew is a fantastical story about a Scarlet Jacobs, who two years prior found herself waking up alone in a forest with no memory of how she got there and who she was. The only recollection she did have was of a symbol she forever doodles all over herself and her shoes. This symbol had to have meant something because it's the only thing she ever remembered of herself or her past. What is more weird is the fact that no one came forward to claim her or even filed out a missing person's report. Alone and scared, if it wasn't for her guardian, Laura and her best friend, Heather, she would be wandering Avalon with no clue. They gave her a chance at a normal life. Until one summer's day at the town's Kissing Festival, her life as she knows it would never be the same again. In walk The Archer Twins. Yes, Tristan (this delicious bad boy has you swooning and sighing) and Gabriel (he irritates me at times but his heart is in the right place) Archer. These twins are hiding something, but little does Scarlet know of the depths of their connection to one another. I mean, there are so many twists and turns in this mysterious story about two brothers and a girl it's so hard not to love the triangle that they are in and it really doesn't determine the story whatsoever. There is enough action and drama to keep you intrigued and excited about turning the page. Most of all, I found myself really investing in the story as well as they characters. Especially Tristan Archer. Oh man, where do I begin with this tortured soul who is so tumultuous and moody, and rude, but at the same time, so sweet and gentle and would do anything for the one's he loves and cares for. The only thing that had me put off at the start was nothing more then the fact that Tristan bares the name of my two sons lol yes, my boys are named Tristan and Archer. But, in saying that, I got over it pretty quick and saw him for who he really was, a character in a story about something fantastical yet so wonderful. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388753129i/7919389._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I absolutely love this book and am grateful to add this to the list of series' I love. I highly recommend those of you who love a great paranormal romance story that is shrouded in mystery and will have you wanting and craving more, just like me. So, take a chance and read it, please! </span>
  <a data-text-id="15263687995533117671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/289214083?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13164574-anew">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=will-probably-regret">will-probably-regret</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=unfinished">unfinished</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289214083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1311952152296777277">I am well and truly sick of unresolved love triangles. The writing of this book is good enough. The characters are strongly presented and the story progresses right along. But I had two problems with the book and they dropped my enjoyment immensely.<br/><br/>First, as I said above, love triangles are completely overdone right now and I just don't feel like tolerating another. I <em>like</em> Gabriel and setting him up against his brother is just cheap. Yeah, you can see they're both sincerely devoted to Scarlet, b</span>
  <span id="freeText1311952152296777277" style="display:none">I am well and truly sick of unresolved love triangles. The writing of this book is good enough. The characters are strongly presented and the story progresses right along. But I had two problems with the book and they dropped my enjoyment immensely.<br /><br />First, as I said above, love triangles are completely overdone right now and I just don't feel like tolerating another. I <em>like</em> Gabriel and setting him up against his brother is just cheap. Yeah, you can see they're both sincerely devoted to Scarlet, but they're also both setup to be the standard driven bad boy vs. kind milquetoast. Ugh.<br /><br />Second, the author is unnaturally coy about elements of the plot. From the first time we meet him, Tristan is trying to end a curse by killing someone. The details of the curse and who he is trying to kill are left completely obscured way past the point of it being mysterious. During one conversation, Tristan cuts a friend off before he gets to the name and that's just cheating. Tristan has no reason to cut him off beyond that the author wants to maintain the "mystery". I got so impatient, I went and read some less-than-discreet reviews just to see what the heck was going on. Seriously, I completely fault the author for that degree of coyness and it completely ruined my desire to finish the book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1311952152296777277" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13340599252652962316" style="display:none">Whaaaaaaaaaat! A book can't end like that! It just can't. <br />Well..it obviously did, but still! That is so mean! <br />Anew was an amazing and incredible ride, if you're looking for a paranormal romance novel. <br />I definitely hate love triangles, but in this case it didn't bother me that much. <div id="review_473653182" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/473653182" />
    <a title="Isha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4738375-isha"><img alt="Isha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589635279p2/4738375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/473653182?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isha" href="/user/show/4738375-isha">Isha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer473653182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7600248280309626042">This book was not what I thought it was going to be, but despite that, I really enjoyed it! Scarlet's past was so unique and interesting to me. I thought the author did a great job of putting the premise together. It drew me in and was a different take on the paranormal stories we usually see.<br/><br/>As far as the characters, I LOVED Tristan. I wish we got more of him in this book or more from his perspective, but I can see him having a bigger role in the future books. I was definitely team Tristan. Gab</span>
  <span id="freeText7600248280309626042" style="display:none">This book was not what I thought it was going to be, but despite that, I really enjoyed it! Scarlet's past was so unique and interesting to me. I thought the author did a great job of putting the premise together. It drew me in and was a different take on the paranormal stories we usually see.<br /><br />As far as the characters, I LOVED Tristan. I wish we got more of him in this book or more from his perspective, but I can see him having a bigger role in the future books. I was definitely team Tristan. Gabriel seemed like a little boy in comparison. Despite him having a bigger role in the book, I just didn't gravitate towards his character. Scarlet was a solid character. As far as side characters go, I wish we got to know more about Laura, Scarlet's guardian. I feel like there were moments where the author hinted at Laura knowing about Scarlet's past, but it was never elaborated on. And then there is Nate. He brought some comic relief to the book and I kind of wish he got to Georgia earlier on in the book, but he was great to read about. And lastly, Heather. I absolutely did not like her. I found her to be annoying and childish.<br /><br />I don't know if I'm going to continue on with this series, mostly because I did find some parts to be slow and I felt like the story was dragging. I also feel like this book would have been great as a New Adult or Adult series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7600248280309626042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mNwesAJxl8aZabpqGhaMPQ71qWzrU/38x0WF5SJntySfshiSnROwqK40M0UgB+RfvjsYPh5bofq1QxGIJugyMg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6eWOMCsDubNpGG8QxAsxQtudxAf6prnzzp5bYPXios/ui4gStGGe3V5F5j/+Glkga1N1VQ+u5fW8mM8N8W0n2Q==')})
  }
//]]>
